# Results of the 2018 Malaysian state elections by constituency

*Source: https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Results_of_the_2018_Malaysian_state_elections_by_constituency*

---

{{Short description|none}}
These are the '''election results of the [[2018 Malaysian general election]] by state constituency'''. [[State legislative assemblies of Malaysia|State assembly]] elections were held in [[Malaysia]] on 9 May 2018 as part of the general elections. Results are expected to come on the same day, after 5 pm. [[List of Malaysian State Assembly Representatives (2018–)|Elected members of the legislative assembly]] (MLAs) will be representing their constituency from the first sitting of respective state legislative assembly to its dissolution.

The state legislature election deposit was set at [[Malaysian ringgit|RM]]5,000 per candidate. Similar to previous elections, the election deposit will be forfeited if the particular candidate had failed to secure at least 12.5% or one-eighth of the votes.
